213→// setEndpointSliceLabels returns a map with the new endpoint slices labels and true if there was an update.\n   214→// Slices labels must be equivalent to the Service labels except for the reserved IsHeadlessService, LabelServiceName and LabelManagedBy labels\n   215→// Changes to IsHeadlessService, LabelServiceName and LabelManagedBy labels on the Service do not result in updates to EndpointSlice labels.\n   216→func setEndpointSliceLabels(logger klog.Logger, epSlice *discovery.EndpointSlice, service *v1.Service, controllerName string) (map[string]string, bool) {\n   217→\tupdated := false\n   218→\tepLabels := make(map[string]string)\n   219→\tsvcLabels := make(map[string]string)\n   220→\n   221→\t// check if the endpoint slice and the service have the same labels\n   222→\t// clone current slice labels except the reserved labels\n   223→\tfor key, value := range epSlice.Labels {\n   224→\t\tif isReservedLabelKey(key) {\n   225→\t\t\tcontinue\n service labels\n   237→\t\tsvcLabels[key] = value\n   238→\t}\n   239→\n   240→\t// if the labels are not identical update the slice with the corresponding service labels\n   241→\tif !apiequality.Semantic.DeepEqual(epLabels, svcLabels) {\n   242→\t\tupdated = true\n   243→\t}\n   244→\n   245→\t// add or remove headless label depending on the service Type\n   246→\tif slices reserved labels\n   253→\tsvcLabels[discovery.LabelServiceName] = service.Name\n   254→\tsvcLabels[discovery.LabelManagedBy] = controllerName\n   255→\n   256→\treturn svcLabels, updated\n   257→}\n   258→\n   259→// isReservedLabelKey return true if the label is one of the reserved label for slices\n   260→func isReservedLabelKey(label string) bool {\n   261→\tif label == 273→func (sl endpointSliceEndpointLen) Len() int      { return len(sl) }\n   274→func (sl endpointSliceEndpointLen) Swap(i, j int) { sl[i], sl[j] = sl[j], sl[i] }\n   275→func (sl
